FILE: mathics/test/builtin/test_comparison.py
FUNCTION: test_unsameq
LINE: 570
INPUT: 2.+ Pi I
EXPECTED: a
MESSAGE: 2. + 3.14159265358979 I == a
NOTE: row `("2.+ Pi I", "a", "2. + 3.14159265358979 I == a")` from
  test_cmp1_no_pass tests `Equal[2.+ Pi I, a]`. Woxi previously kept
  `Pi` symbolic in `2. + Pi I` (returned `2. + I*Pi == a`); fixed Plus
  to numerify named constants (Pi, E, Sqrt[2], ...) and any constants
  embedded in otherwise-symbolic summands when at least one summand is
  a machine Real, so `2.+ Pi I` now evaluates to
  `2. + 3.141592653589793*I` (matches wolframscript). The mathics
  expected `…3.14159265358979 I` truncates one digit; the EXPECTED is
  still effectively equivalent for the structural Equal test.
  Regression tests: tests/interpreter_tests/arithmetic.rs::
  plus_numeric_contagion::*.

FILE: mathics/test/builtin/test_procedural.py
FUNCTION: test_history_compound_expression
LINE: 127
INPUT: ToString[%]
EXPECTED: y
NOTE: tests REPL/CLI `%` semantics: after `CompoundExpression[x, y, Null]`
  in a fresh REPL cell, `Out[n]` and `%` reference the last non-Null
  element (`y`), not the actual `Null` return value. Real wolframscript
  REPL produces `y` here (verified via stdin REPL test). However in
  *script* mode (both `wolframscript -code` / `-file` and Woxi's `eval`
  / `run`), `%` collapses to `Out[0]` because there is no per-cell
  Out-history. Woxi's command-line `eval` therefore matches
  wolframscript's script-mode behavior (`Out[0]`), not its REPL
  behavior. Implementing this test requires REPL/notebook support,
  which is out of scope here. See `src/lib.rs` `set_last_output` (gated
  on `VISUAL_MODE`) for the infrastructure that already exists for
  woxi-studio's notebook mode.
---

INPUT: ToString[%]
EXPECTED: x
NOTE: REPL-only — same family as line 127. After
  `CompoundExpression[CompoundExpression[y, x, Null], Null]` in a REPL,
  `%` stores the last non-Null sub-expression (`x`). Woxi script-mode
  `eval` resolves `%` to `Out[0]`, matching wolframscript script mode.
  See memory `project-woxi-no-repl-history`.

FILE: mathics/test/builtin/numbers/test_randomnumbers.py
FUNCTION: None
LINE: 14
INPUT: SeedRandom[42]; RandomSample[{a, b, c, d}]
EXPECTED: {b, d, a, c}
NOTE: RNG-sequence divergence. mathics's expected `{b, d, a, c}` is
  Python's `random` output for seed 42. Real wolframscript produces
  `{b, c, d, a}`; Woxi (ChaCha8Rng) produces `{a, c, b, d}`. All three
  return valid 4-element permutations of `{a, b, c, d}` and are
  deterministic for a fixed seed, but the exact ordering depends on
  the underlying RNG. Implementing wolframscript-byte-equivalent RNG
  is out of scope. See memory `project-rng-sequence-divergence`.
